Here is a code you can use as a crewmate in Mira HQ using the doors to the balcony/satellite dish when you are a ghost:  1. Make sure an alive crewmate is near the doors. 2.Go from the cafeteria to the balcony using the doors. 3 Repeat step 2 the number of time the  impostor is on the emergency meetings list.  Now the alive crewmate will know what is the place the impostor is on the list by checking the number of times you go in and out of the doors.  For example:  If yellow is the impostor, then wait until an emergency meeting starts. Check the place where yellow (the impostor) is on the list. (lets take it if he's the fourth on the list.) Then make sure an alive crewmate is near the doors. Go from the cafeteria to the balcony using the door 4 (the place where yellow(the impostor) is on the list.) times.  Now the alive crewmate will know what is the place the impostor is on the list by checking the number of times you go in and out of the doors.    So now when a meeting pops up, the crewmate will know what place to check. (In this case place 4 the place of yellow)  Then he'll tell yellow is the impostor to everyone in the chat.

The Bait (epic impostor strat):  Make sure there is a person in a specific place the admin table registers.  Be in that place. DO NOT kill the person inside. This is important.  Make sure someone is at admin table looking for blink kills. I'll mention this later.  Now, be close to the hallway, if you're in hallways, admin table won't see you. Make sure you're a centimeter before the hallway.  Now, step outside for a millisecond and immediately go back in. Make sure the person leaves and you're still inside.  The person at admin will notice two people and one dissapeared and reappeared. This counts as a body.  And then, once they come inside, they'll report a body that has never been there.  It's your chance to kill that person and lock doors.    A blink kill is a kill that happens inside a place that is registered in the admin table, if you kill, or you get killed, the admin table will show one person dissapearing and reappearing. The one is a body, the other is an impostor. If the killer dissapears, they might appear in another location which means they vented.  If I got anything wrong, correct me in the comments.
